        function redirectBackOrHome(fallbackUrl) {
            fallbackUrl = fallbackUrl || '/';
            var prevPage = location.href;

            if (self.history.length > 2) {
                // chrome has 2 elements per default
                self.history.back();
            } else {
                self.location.href = fallbackUrl;
            }
        }
